< Text>
1st time at this place. Visited while we were on vacation in Palm Desert. I was surprised at the amazingly fresh fare. It tasted like we were seaside instead of being in the middle of a desert. Great tasting sushi. One bit of criticism, I ordered the Hatari Pork bun and was very dry despite the generous amount of sauce. But all in all a surprise considering it was in a tourist trap location.  It outperformed its surroundings.<//Text>

< text>
Unbelievably good sushi. Sashimi was fresh as the rolls were big, and not because they padded then with rice.

We got takeout in the middle of the pandemic restrictions and the food was ready in less than 30 minutes and the staff on the phone and in person could not have been kinder.

I highly recommend Happy Sushi, you will not be disappointed.<//text>

<Review>I had a craving for Ramen and I went for the Ramen. I ordered the Spicy Miso Ramen, and must say, I have had way better instant Ramen, Nissin makes a better noodle and broth than this place. The veggies were either from frozen packs or canned, the broth had an overpowering ginger flavor. The spiciness in the spicy miso must have originated from a bottle of shriracha or a similar chili garlic sauce because it added a sweet flavor. The Nori was the slick texture or instant miso soup. Which explains allot of my gripe about the ramen. The noodles we're too soft no spring to them and very short, I couldn't perform the customary slurping as the noodle had no length to reach the edge of the liquids surface as dangling from my mouth. My biggest issue the egg, it was hardboiled, and the yolk was over done so it became powdery and polluted the soup base. In addition I ordered a Salmon skin salad, it wasn't good either, and it came after I finished my Ramen. Salad regardless of type should be served as a starter, and if that's not the case at your establishment inform the customer. I will never be going here again.<//Review>< Date>

< review>
A large park, with two great kids play areas with lots of fun equipment (especially for middle aged kids). There are paved paths to walk or skate. There are four large baseball fields with impeccably manicured grass and great seats.

There is lots of parking spots all around the park.</review>

In addition to the bathrooms which as accessbile, there's a ceramic art studio which has been closed during the pandemic. Lastly for dog lovers, Cupertino parks provides bags for everyone to pick up after their pets.</review>< pics>

< Text>
Often difficult to navigate, Terminal 5, as all terminals in LAX, can be a bit of a trick. But Hawaiian Airlines and American airlines that fly out of this terminal are good services and there are a lot of amenities to tide your time as you wait. See's candy, I love LA, and Skewers by Muramoto are within the terminal. If these don't satisfy, and you have a lot of time on your hands, in the next terminal by walkway are Dunkin Donuts, Umami Burger LAX, and Rock & Brews. There are power stations setup through the terminal so you can charge your device. But they get filled quickly, so when you see a spot open take it. And this way you can enjoy working on your tablet or listening to music or watching a video while you wait, and you can still be charged up and ready to go when you board your plane. Enjoy your trip.<//Text>

Their menu is different from what you see online - no tacos and only salmon/tuna/shrimp from the seafood options. No catch of the day neither. I had crab cakes-one of very few seafood options; and  hot chicken biscuit. Seemed like crab cakes is not a popular item - took awhile to arrive, actually the side dish it came with was amazing, crabcakes itself - okay, too mushy to my taste. Hot chicken biscut was great (came with fries). Biscuit was perfectly warm and slightly crunchy on the outside, but soft inside. Fried chicken was juicy and well seasoned - not too spicy though. Nice variety of drinks available - craft local beers, wines and selections of good quality spirits.< /text>

<Text>OB Surf Lodge is "good enough." The service was good and the location was great; can't beat the ocean view. The food itself is good, just nothing worth getting excited about. I had the Carnitas Benny; which is eggs Benedict with Carnitas on top of what I think was an English muffin. The muffin was flat and a bit rough l, Soni couldn't really tell what it was. I had a mimosa flight. It came with 4 kinds of mimosa. They were decent enough, but you could taste the syrup. I'd come back if only for the atmosphere, but there are better brunch spots in OB.</Text>< pictures>

< Review>
My husband and I had our first date here when it was Shades in April 2007. We love the ocean view, the surfers, the dogs, and all the local color. It's our special place. The new management seems to have captured the essence of this sacred OB space - right on the water, next to the OB Pier, casual but elegant too. It's a bit pricier than it use to be - Bloody Mary's were $10 each, breakfast was $15 each, and a $50 dollar bill after we looked up from the waves. It didn't use to cost that! Nonetheless, we always go to this spot when we're visiting San Diego from the Palm Springs desert area. The OB Pier is our special spot. I just wish the new management had a drink special for us budget travelers. We shouldn't have to carry an AMEX card to go here.  This is OB man!< /Review>

<Review>My husband and I had our first date here when it was Shades in April 2007. We love the ocean view, the surfers, the dogs, and all the local color. It's our special place. The new management seems to have captured the essence of this sacred OB space - right on the water, next to the OB Pier, casual but elegant too. It's a bit pricier than it use to be - Bloody Mary's were $10 each, breakfast was $15 each, and a $50 dollar bill after we looked up from the waves. It didn't use to cost that! Nonetheless, we always go to this spot when we're visiting San Diego from the Palm Springs desert area. The OB Pier is our special spot. I just wish the new management had a drink special for us budget travelers. We shouldn't have to carry an AMEX card to go here.  This is OB man!<//Review>< gmapID>
